I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
WKT1-based transformation fails while same proj4-based trans succeeds
I'm having trouble with `NaN`s produced in transformation with this WKT2 CRS from a MODIS image:

```js
const proj4 = require("proj4") // v2.20.2

const sourceCrs = 'PROJCS["unnamed",GEOGCS["Unknown datum based upon the custom spheroid",DATUM["Not specified (based on custom spheroid)",SPHEROID["Custom spheroid",6371007.181,0]],PRIMEM["Greenwich",0],UNIT["degree",0.0174532925199433,AUTHORITY["EPSG","9122"]]],PROJECTION["Sinusoidal"],PARAMETER["longitude_of_center",0],PARAMETER["false_easting",0],PARAMETER["false_northing",0],UNIT["Meter",1],AXIS["Easting",EAST],AXIS["Northing",NORTH]]'

const converter = proj4(sourceCrs, "EPSG:4326");
console.log(converter.forward([-8895604.157333, 4447802.078667]));
// [NaN, NaN]
```

In Python, it works well:

```py
from pyproj import Transformer

crs = 'PROJCS["unnamed",GEOGCS["Unknown datum based upon the custom spheroid",DATUM["Not specified (based on custom spheroid)",SPHEROID["Custom spheroid",6371007.181,0]],PRIMEM["Greenwich",0],UNIT["degree",0.0174532925199433,AUTHORITY["EPSG","9122"]]],PROJECTION["Sinusoidal"],PARAMETER["longitude_of_center",0],PARAMETER["false_easting",0],PARAMETER["false_northing",0],UNIT["Meter",1],AXIS["Easting",EAST],AXIS["Northing",NORTH]]'

transformer = Transformer.from_crs(crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
transformer.transform(-8895604.157333, 4447802.078667)
# (-104.43258313171073, 39.99999999641088)
```

If I use what pyproj says is the relevant proj4 string, it works well:

```py
from pyproj import CRS
CRS(crs).to_proj4()
# '+proj=sinu +lon_0=0 +x_0=0 +y_0=0 +R=6371007.181 +units=m +no_defs +type=crs'
```

```js
const proj4 = require("proj4") // v2.20.2

const sourceCrs = '+proj=sinu +lon_0=0 +x_0=0 +y_0=0 +R=6371007.181 +units=m +no_defs +type=crs';

const converter = proj4(sourceCrs, "EPSG:4326");
console.log(converter.forward([-8895604.157333, 4447802.078667]));
// [-104.43258313171073, 39.99999999641088]
```

     1	import { SIXTH, RA4, RA6, EPSLN } from './constants/values';
     2	import { default as Ellipsoid } from './constants/Ellipsoid';
     3	import match from './match';
     4	
     5	const WGS84 = Ellipsoid.WGS84; // default ellipsoid
     6	
     7	export function eccentricity(a, b, rf, R_A) {
     8	  var a2 = a * a; // used in geocentric
     9	  var b2 = b * b; // used in geocentric
    10	  var es = (a2 - b2) / a2; // e ^ 2
    11	  var e = 0;
    12	  if (R_A) {
    13	    a *= 1 - es * (SIXTH + es * (RA4 + es * RA6));
    14	    a2 = a * a;
    15	    es = 0;
    16	  } else {
    17	    e = Math.sqrt(es); // eccentricity
    18	  }
    19	  var ep2 = (a2 - b2) / b2; // used in geocentric
    20	  return {
    21	    es: es,
    22	    e: e,
    23	    ep2: ep2
    24	  };
    25	}
    26	export function sphere(a, b, rf, ellps, sphere) {
    27	  if (!a) { // do we have an ellipsoid?
    28	    var ellipse = match(Ellipsoid, ellps);
    29	    if (!ellipse) {
    30	      ellipse = WGS84;
    31	    }
    32	    a = ellipse.a;
    33	    b = ellipse.b;
    34	    rf = ellipse.rf;
    35	  }
    36	
    37	  if (rf && !b) {
    38	    b = (1.0 - 1.0 / rf) * a;
    39	  }
    40	  if (rf === 0 || Math.abs(a - b) < EPSLN) {
    41	    sphere = true;
    42	    b = a;
    43	  }
    44	  return {
    45	    a: a,
    46	    b: b,
    47	    rf: rf,
    48	    sphere: sphere
    49	  };
    50	}
    51

    10	/**
    11	 * @typedef {Object} DatumDefinition
    12	 * @property {number} datum_type - The type of datum.
    13	 * @property {number} a - Semi-major axis of the ellipsoid.
    14	 * @property {number} b - Semi-minor axis of the ellipsoid.
    15	 * @property {number} es - Eccentricity squared of the ellipsoid.

    19	/**
    20	 * @param {string | import('./core').PROJJSONDefinition | import('./defs').ProjectionDefinition} srsCode
    21	 * @param {(errorMessage?: string, instance?: Projection) => void} [callback]
    22	 */
    23	function Projection(srsCode, callback) {
    24	  if (!(this instanceof Projection)) {
    25	    return new Projection(srsCode);
    26	  }
    27	  /** @type {<T extends import('./core').TemplateCoordinates>(coordinates: T, enforceAxis?: boolean) => T} */
    28	  this.forward = null;
    29	  /** @type {<T extends import('./core').TemplateCoordinates>(coordinates: T, enforceAxis?: boolean) => T} */
    30	  this.inverse = null;
    31	  /** @type {function(): void} */
    32	  this.init = null;
    33	  /** @type {string} */
    34	  this.name;
    35	  /** @type {Array<string>} */
    36	  this.names = null;
    37	  /** @type {string} */
    38	  this.title;
    39	  callback = callback || function (error) {
    40	    if (error) {
    41	      throw error;
    42	    }
    43	  };
    44	  var json = parseCode(srsCode);
    45	  if (typeof json !== 'object') {
    46	    callback('Could not parse to valid json: ' + srsCode);
    47	    return;
    48	  }
    49	  var ourProj = Projection.projections.get(json.projName);
    50	  if (!ourProj) {
    51	    callback('Could not get projection name from: ' + srsCode);
    52	    return;
    53	  }
    54	  if (json.datumCode && json.datumCode !== 'none') {
    55	    var datumDef = match(Datum, json.datumCode);
    56	    if (datumDef) {
    57	      json.datum_params = json.datum_params || (datumDef.towgs84 ? datumDef.towgs84.split(',') : null);
    58	      json.ellps = datumDef.ellipse;
    59	      json.datumName = datumDef.datumName ? datumDef.datumName : json.datumCode;
    60	    }
    61	  }
    62	  json.k0 = json.k0 || 1.0;
    63	  json.axis = json.axis || 'enu';
    64	  json.ellps = json.ellps || 'wgs84';
    65	  json.lat1 = json.lat1 || json.lat0; // Lambert_Conformal_Conic_1SP, for example, needs this
    66	
    67	  var sphere_ = dc_sphere(json.a, json.b, json.rf, json.ellps, json.sphere);
    68	  var ecc = dc_eccentricity(sphere_.a, sphere_.b, sphere_.rf, json.R_A);
    69	  var nadgrids = getNadgrids(json.nadgrids);
    70	  /** @type {DatumDefinition} */
    71	  var datumObj = json.datum || datum(json.datumCode, json.datum_params, sphere_.a, sphere_.b, ecc.es, ecc.ep2,
    72	    nadgrids);
    73	
    74	  extend(this, json); // transfer everything over from the projection because we don't know what we'll need
    75	  extend(this, ourProj); // transfer all the methods from the projection
    76	
    77	  // copy the 4 things over we calculated in deriveConstants.sphere
    78	  this.a = sphere_.a;
    79	  this.b = sphere_.b;
    80	  this.rf = sphere_.rf;
    81	  this.sphere = sphere_.sphere;
    82

    84	  this.es = ecc.es;
    85	  this.e = ecc.e;
    86	  this.ep2 = ecc.ep2;
    87	
    88	  // add in the datum object
    89	  this.datum = datumObj;
    90	
    91	  // init the projection
    92	  if ('init' in this && typeof this.init === 'function') {
    93	    this.init();
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  // legecy callback from back in the day when it went to spatialreference.org
    97	  callback(null, this);
    98	}

     1	import adjust_lon from '../common/adjust_lon';
     2	import adjust_lat from '../common/adjust_lat';
     3	import pj_enfn from '../common/pj_enfn';
     4	var MAX_ITER = 20;
     5	import pj_mlfn from '../common/pj_mlfn';
     6	import pj_inv_mlfn from '../common/pj_inv_mlfn';
     7	import { EPSLN, HALF_PI } from '../constants/values';
     8	
     9	import asinz from '../common/asinz';
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * @typedef {Object} LocalThis
    13	 * @property {Array<number>} en
    14	 * @property {number} n
    15	 * @property {number} m
    16	 * @property {number} C_y
    17	 * @property {number} C_x
    18	 * @property {number} es
    19	 */
    20	
    21	/** @this {import('../defs.js').ProjectionDefinition & LocalThis} */
    22	export function init() {
    23	  /* Place parameters in static storage for common use
    24	    ------------------------------------------------- */
    25	
    26	  if (!this.sphere) {
    27	    this.en = pj_enfn(this.es);
    28	  } else {
    29	    this.n = 1;
    30	    this.m = 0;
    31	    this.es = 0;
    32	    this.C_y = Math.sqrt((this.m + 1) / this.n);
    33	    this.C_x = this.C_y / (this.m + 1);
    34	  }
    35	}
    36	
    37	/* Sinusoidal forward equations--mapping lat,long to x,y
    38	  ----------------------------------------------------- */
    39	export function forward(p) {
    40	  var x, y;
    41	  var lon = p.x;
    42	  var lat = p.y;
    43	  /* Forward equations
    44	    ----------------- */
    45	  lon = adjust_lon(lon - this.long0, this.over);
    46	
    47	  if (this.sphere) {
    48	    if (!this.m) {
    49	      lat = this.n !== 1 ? Math.asin(this.n * Math.sin(lat)) : lat;
    50	    } else {
    51	      var k = this.n * Math.sin(lat);
    52	      for (var i = MAX_ITER; i; --i) {
    53	        var V = (this.m * lat + Math.sin(lat) - k) / (this.m + Math.cos(lat));
    54	        lat -= V;
    55	        if (Math.abs(V) < EPSLN) {
    56	          break;
    57	        }
    58	      }
    59	    }
    60	    x = this.a * this.C_x * lon * (this.m + Math.cos(lat));
    61	    y = this.a * this.C_y * lat;
    62	  } else {
    63	    var s = Math.sin(lat);
    64	    var c = Math.cos(lat);
    65	    y = this.a * pj_mlfn(lat, s, c, this.en);
    66	    x = this.a * lon * c / Math.sqrt(1 - this.es * s * s);
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  p.x = x;
    70	  p.y = y;
    71	  return p;
    72	}
    73	
    74	export function inverse(p) {
    75	  var lat, temp, lon, s;
    76	
    77	  p.x -= this.x0;
    78	  lon = p.x / this.a;
    79	  p.y -= this.y0;
    80	  lat = p.y / this.a;
    81	
    82	  if (this.sphere) {
    83	    lat /= this.C_y;
    84	    lon = lon / (this.C_x * (this.m + Math.cos(lat)));
    85	    if (this.m) {
    86	      lat = asinz((this.m * lat + Math.sin(lat)) / this.n);
    87	    } else if (this.n !== 1) {
    88	      lat = asinz(Math.sin(lat) / this.n);
    89	    }
    90	    lon = adjust_lon(lon + this.long0, this.over);
    91	    lat = adjust_lat(lat);
    92	  } else {
    93	    lat = pj_inv_mlfn(p.y / this.a, this.es, this.en);
    94	    s = Math.abs(lat);
    95	    if (s < HALF_PI) {
    96	      s = Math.sin(lat);
    97	      temp = this.long0 + p.x * Math.sqrt(1 - this.es * s * s) / (this.a * Math.cos(lat));
    98	      // temp = this.long0 + p.x / (this.a * Math.cos(lat));
    99	      lon = adjust_lon(temp, this.over);
   100	    } else if ((s - EPSLN) < HALF_PI) {
   101	      lon = this.long0;
   102	    }
   103	  }
   104	  p.x = lon;
   105	  p.y = lat;
   106	  return p;
   107	}
   108	
   109	export var names = ['Sinusoidal', 'sinu'];
   110	export default {
   111	  init: init,
   112	  forward: forward,
   113	  inverse: inverse,
   114	  names: names
   115	};

     1	import defs from './defs';
     2	import wkt from 'wkt-parser';
     3	import projStr from './projString';
     4	import match from './match';
     5	function testObj(code) {
     6	  return typeof code === 'string';
     7	}
     8	function testDef(code) {
     9	  return code in defs;
    10	}
    11	function testWKT(code) {
    12	  return (code.indexOf('+') !== 0 && code.indexOf('[') !== -1) || (typeof code === 'object' && !('srsCode' in code));
    13	}
    14	var codes = ['3857', '900913', '3785', '102113'];
    15	function checkMercator(item) {
    16	  if (item.title) {
    17	    return item.title.toLowerCase().indexOf('epsg:') === 0 && codes.indexOf(item.title.substr(5)) > -1;
    18	  }
    19	  var auth = match(item, 'authority');
    20	  if (!auth) {
    21	    return;
    22	  }
    23	  var code = match(auth, 'epsg');
    24	  return code && codes.indexOf(code) > -1;
    25	}
    26	function checkProjStr(item) {
    27	  var ext = match(item, 'extension');
    28	  if (!ext) {
    29	    return;
    30	  }
    31	  return match(ext, 'proj4');
    32	}
    33	function testProj(code) {
    34	  return code[0] === '+';
    35	}
    36	/**
    37	 * @param {string | import('./core').PROJJSONDefinition | import('./defs').ProjectionDefinition} code
    38	 * @returns {import('./defs').ProjectionDefinition}
    39	 */
    40	function parse(code) {
    41	  let out;
    42	  if (testObj(code)) {
    43	    // check to see if this is a WKT string
    44	    if (testDef(code)) {
    45	      out = defs[code];
    46	    } else if (testWKT(code)) {
    47	      out = wkt(code);
    48	      var maybeProjStr = checkProjStr(out);
    49	      if (maybeProjStr) {
    50	        out = projStr(maybeProjStr);
    51	      }
    52	    } else if (testProj(code)) {
    53	      out = projStr(code);
    54	    }
    55	  } else if (!('projName' in code)) {
    56	    out = wkt(code);
    57	  } else {
    58	    out = code;
    59	  }
    60	  // test for special Web Mercator case, due to this being a very common and often malformed
    61	  return out && checkMercator(out) ? defs['EPSG:3857'] : out;
    62	}
    63	
    64	export default parse;
    65

     2	
     3	export function d2r(input) {
     4	  return input * D2R;
     5	}
     6	
     7	export function applyProjectionDefaults(wkt) {
     8	  // Normalize projName for WKT2 compatibility
     9	  const normalizedProjName = (wkt.projName || '').toLowerCase().replace(/_/g, ' ');
    10	
    11	  if (!wkt.long0 && wkt.longc && (normalizedProjName === 'albers conic equal area' || normalizedProjName === 'lambert azimuthal equal area')) {
    12	    wkt.long0 = wkt.longc;
    13	  }
    14	  if (!wkt.lat_ts && wkt.lat1 && (normalizedProjName === 'stereographic south pole' || normalizedProjName === 'polar stereographic (variant b)')) {
    15	    wkt.lat0 = d2r(wkt.lat1 > 0 ? 90 : -90);
    16	    wkt.lat_ts = wkt.lat1;
    17	    delete wkt.lat1;
    18	  } else if (!wkt.lat_ts && wkt.lat0 && (normalizedProjName === 'polar stereographic' || normalizedProjName === 'polar stereographic (variant a)')) {

    22	  }

     2	 * Copyright 2018 Bernie Jenny, Monash University, Melbourne, Australia.

    13	 * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
    14	 * limitations under the License.
    15	 *
    16	 * Equal Earth is a projection inspired by the Robinson projection, but unlike
    17	 * the Robinson projection retains the relative size of areas. The projection
    18	 * was designed in 2018 by Bojan Savric, Tom Patterson and Bernhard Jenny.
    19	 *
    20	 * Publication:
    21	 * Bojan Savric, Tom Patterson & Bernhard Jenny (2018). The Equal Earth map
    22	 * projection, International Journal of Geographical Information Science,
    23	 * DOI: 10.1080/13658816.2018.1504949
    24	 *
    25	 * Code released August 2018
    26	 * Ported to JavaScript and adapted for mapshaper-proj by Matthew Bloch August 2018
    27	 * Modified for proj4js by Andreas Hocevar by Andreas Hocevar March 2024
    28	 */
    29	
    30	import adjust_lon from '../common/adjust_lon';
    31	
    32	var A1 = 1.340264,
    33	  A2 = -0.081106,
    34	  A3 = 0.000893,
    35	  A4 = 0.003796,
    36	  M = Math.sqrt(3) / 2.0;
    37	
    38	export function init() {
    39	  this.es = 0;
    40	  this.long0 = this.long0 !== undefined ? this.long0 : 0;
    41	  this.x0 = this.x0 !== undefined ? this.x0 : 0;
    42	  this.y0 = this.y0 !== undefined ? this.y0 : 0;
    43	}
    44	
    45	export function forward(p) {
    46	  var lam = adjust_lon(p.x - this.long0, this.over);
    47	  var phi = p.y;
    48	  var paramLat = Math.asin(M * Math.sin(phi)),
    49	    paramLatSq = paramLat * paramLat,
    50	    paramLatPow6 = paramLatSq * paramLatSq * paramLatSq;
    51	  p.x = lam * Math.cos(paramLat)
    52	    / (M * (A1 + 3 * A2 * paramLatSq + paramLatPow6 * (7 * A3 + 9 * A4 * paramLatSq)));
    53	  p.y = paramLat * (A1 + A2 * paramLatSq + paramLatPow6 * (A3 + A4 * paramLatSq));
    54	
    55	  p.x = this.a * p.x + this.x0;
    56	  p.y = this.a * p.y + this.y0;
    57	  return p;
    58	}
    59	
    60	export function inverse(p) {
    61	  p.x = (p.x - this.x0) / this.a;
    62	  p.y = (p.y - this.y0) / this.a;
    63	
    64	  var EPS = 1e-9,
    65	    NITER = 12,
    66	    paramLat = p.y,
    67	    paramLatSq, paramLatPow6, fy, fpy, dlat, i;
    68	
    69	  for (i = 0; i < NITER; ++i) {
    70	    paramLatSq = paramLat * paramLat;
    71	    paramLatPow6 = paramLatSq * paramLatSq * paramLatSq;
    72	    fy = paramLat * (A1 + A2 * paramLatSq + paramLatPow6 * (A3 + A4 * paramLatSq)) - p.y;
    73	    fpy = A1 + 3 * A2 * paramLatSq + paramLatPow6 * (7 * A3 + 9 * A4 * paramLatSq);
    74	    paramLat -= dlat = fy / fpy;
    75	    if (Math.abs(dlat) < EPS) {
    76	      break;
    77	    }
    78	  }
    79	  paramLatSq = paramLat * paramLat;
    80	  paramLatPow6 = paramLatSq * paramLatSq * paramLatSq;
    81	  p.x = M * p.x * (A1 + 3 * A2 * paramLatSq + paramLatPow6 * (7 * A3 + 9 * A4 * paramLatSq))
    82	    / Math.cos(paramLat);
    83	  p.y = Math.asin(Math.sin(paramLat) / M);
    84	
    85	  p.x = adjust_lon(p.x + this.long0, this.over);
    86	  return p;
    87	}
    88	
    89	export var names = ['eqearth', 'Equal Earth', 'Equal_Earth'];
    90	export default {
    91	  init: init,
    92	  forward: forward,
    93	  inverse: inverse,
    94	  names: names
    95	};

     1	import { PJD_3PARAM, PJD_7PARAM, PJD_GRIDSHIFT, PJD_WGS84, PJD_NODATUM, SEC_TO_RAD } from './constants/values';
     2	
     3	function datum(datumCode, datum_params, a, b, es, ep2, nadgrids) {
     4	  var out = {};
     5	
     6	  if (datumCode === undefined || datumCode === 'none') {
     7	    out.datum_type = PJD_NODATUM;
     8	  } else {
     9	    out.datum_type = PJD_WGS84;
    10	  }
    11	
    12	  if (datum_params) {
    13	    out.datum_params = datum_params.map(parseFloat);
    14	    if (out.datum_params[0] !== 0 || out.datum_params[1] !== 0 || out.datum_params[2] !== 0) {
    15	      out.datum_type = PJD_3PARAM;
    16	    }
    17	    if (out.datum_params.length > 3) {
    18	      if (out.datum_params[3] !== 0 || out.datum_params[4] !== 0 || out.datum_params[5] !== 0 || out.datum_params[6] !== 0) {
    19	        out.datum_type = PJD_7PARAM;
    20	        out.datum_params[3] *= SEC_TO_RAD;
    21	        out.datum_params[4] *= SEC_TO_RAD;
    22	        out.datum_params[5] *= SEC_TO_RAD;
    23	        out.datum_params[6] = (out.datum_params[6] / 1000000.0) + 1.0;
    24	      }
    25	    }
    26	  }
    27	
    28	  if (nadgrids) {
    29	    out.datum_type = PJD_GRIDSHIFT;
    30	    out.grids = nadgrids;
    31	  }
    32	  out.a = a; // datum object also uses these values
    33	  out.b = b;
    34	  out.es = es;
    35	  out.ep2 = ep2;
    36	  return out;
    37	}
    38	
    39	export default datum;

     1	import {
     2	  PJD_3PARAM,
     3	  PJD_7PARAM,
     4	  PJD_GRIDSHIFT,
     5	  PJD_NODATUM,
     6	  R2D,
     7	  SRS_WGS84_ESQUARED,
     8	  SRS_WGS84_SEMIMAJOR, SRS_WGS84_SEMIMINOR
     9	} from './constants/values';
    10	
    11	import { geodeticToGeocentric, geocentricToGeodetic, geocentricToWgs84, geocentricFromWgs84, compareDatums } from './datumUtils';
    12	import adjust_lon from './common/adjust_lon';
    13	function checkParams(type) {
    14	  return (type === PJD_3PARAM || type === PJD_7PARAM);
    15	}
    16	
    17	export default function (source, dest, point) {
    18	  // Short cut if the datums are identical.
    19	  if (compareDatums(source, dest)) {
    20	    return point; // in this case, zero is sucess,
    21	    // whereas cs_compare_datums returns 1 to indicate TRUE
    22	    // confusing, should fix this
    23	  }
    24	
    25	  // Explicitly skip datum transform by setting 'datum=none' as parameter for either source or dest
    26	  if (source.datum_type === PJD_NODATUM || dest.datum_type === PJD_NODATUM) {
    27	    return point;
    28	  }
    29	
    30	  // If this datum requires grid shifts, then apply it to geodetic coordinates.
    31	  var source_a = source.a;
    32	  var source_es = source.es;
    33	  if (source.datum_type === PJD_GRIDSHIFT) {
    34	    var gridShiftCode = applyGridShift(source, false, point);
    35	    if (gridShiftCode !== 0) {
    36	      return undefined;
    37	    }
    38	    source_a = SRS_WGS84_SEMIMAJOR;
    39	    source_es = SRS_WGS84_ESQUARED;
    40	  }
    41	
    42	  var dest_a = dest.a;
    43	  var dest_b = dest.b;
    44	  var dest_es = dest.es;
    45	  if (dest.datum_type === PJD_GRIDSHIFT) {
    46	    dest_a = SRS_WGS84_SEMIMAJOR;
    47	    dest_b = SRS_WGS84_SEMIMINOR;
    48	    dest_es = SRS_WGS84_ESQUARED;
    49	  }
    50	
    51	  // Do we need to go through geocentric coordinates?
    52	  if (source_es === dest_es && source_a === dest_a && !checkParams(source.datum_type) && !checkParams(dest.datum_type)) {
    53	    return point;
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  // Convert to geocentric coordinates.
    57	  point = geodeticToGeocentric(point, source_es, source_a);
    58	  // Convert between datums
    59	  if (checkParams(source.datum_type)) {
    60	    point = geocentricToWgs84(point, source.datum_type, source.datum_params);
    61	  }
    62	  if (checkParams(dest.datum_type)) {
    63	    point = geocentricFromWgs84(point, dest.datum_type, dest.datum_params);
    64	  }
    65	  point = geocentricToGeodetic(point, dest_es, dest_a, dest_b);
    66	
    67	  if (dest.datum_type === PJD_GRIDSHIFT) {
    68	    var destGridShiftResult = applyGridShift(dest, true, point);
    69	    if (destGridShiftResult !== 0) {
    70	      return undefined;
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return point;
    75	}
    76	
    77	export function applyGridShift(source, inverse, point) {
    78	  if (source.grids === null || source.grids.length === 0) {
    79	    console.log('Grid shift grids not found');
    80	    return -1;
    81	  }
    82	  var input = { x: -point.x, y: point.y };
    83	  var output = { x: Number.NaN, y: Number.NaN };
    84	  var attemptedGrids = [];
    85	  outer:
    86	  for (var i = 0; i < source.grids.length; i++) {
    87	    var grid = source.grids[i];
    88	    attemptedGrids.push(grid.name);
    89	    if (grid.isNull) {
    90	      output = input;
    91	      break;
    92	    }
    93	    if (grid.grid === null) {
    94	      if (grid.mandatory) {
    95	        console.log('Unable to find mandatory grid \'' + grid.name + '\'');
    96	        return -1;
    97	      }
    98	      continue;
    99	    }
   100	    var subgrids = grid.grid.subgrids;
   101	    for (var j = 0, jj = subgrids.length; j < jj; j++) {
   102	      var subgrid = subgrids[j];
   103	      // skip tables that don't match our point at all
   104	      var epsilon = (Math.abs(subgrid.del[1]) + Math.abs(subgrid.del[0])) / 10000.0;
   105	      var minX = subgrid.ll[0] - epsilon;
   106	      var minY = subgrid.ll[1] - epsilon;
   107	      var maxX = subgrid.ll[0] + (subgrid.lim[0] - 1) * subgrid.del[0] + epsilon;
   108	      var maxY = subgrid.ll[1] + (subgrid.lim[1] - 1) * subgrid.del[1] + epsilon;
   109	      if (minY > input.y || minX > input.x || maxY < input.y || maxX < input.x) {
   110	        continue;
   111	      }
   112	      output = applySubgridShift(input, inverse, subgrid);
   113	      if (!isNaN(output.x)) {
   114	        break outer;
   115	      }
   116	    }
   117	  }
   118	  if (isNaN(output.x)) {
   119	    console.log('Failed to find a grid shift table for location \''
   120	      + -input.x * R2D + ' ' + input.y * R2D + ' tried: \'' + attemptedGrids + '\'');
   121	    return -1;
   122	  }
   123	  point.x = -output.x;
   124	  point.y = output.y;
   125	  return 0;
   126	}
   127	
   128	function applySubgridShift(pin, inverse, ct) {
   129	  var val = { x: Number.NaN, y: Number.NaN };
   130	  if (isNaN(pin.x)) {
   131	    return val;
   132	  }
   133	  var tb = { x: pin.x, y: pin.y };
   134	  tb.x -= ct.ll[0];
   135	  tb.y -= ct.ll[1];
   136	  tb.x = adjust_lon(tb.x - Math.PI) + Math.PI;
   137	  var t = nadInterpolate(tb, ct);
   138	  if (inverse) {
   139	    if (isNaN(t.x)) {
   140	      return val;
   141	    }
   142	    t.x = tb.x - t.x;
   143	    t.y = tb.y - t.y;
   144	    var i = 9, tol = 1e-12;
   145	    var dif, del;
   146	    do {
   147	      del = nadInterpolate(t, ct);
   148	      if (isNaN(del.x)) {
   149	        console.log('Inverse grid shift iteration failed, presumably at grid edge.  Using first approximation.');
   150	        break;
   151	      }
   152	      dif = { x: tb.x - (del.x + t.x), y: tb.y - (del.y + t.y) };
   153	      t.x += dif.x;
   154	      t.y += dif.y;
   155	    } while (i-- && Math.abs(dif.x) > tol && Math.abs(dif.y) > tol);
   156	    if (i < 0) {
   157	      console.log('Inverse grid shift iterator failed to converge.');
   158	      return val;
   159	    }
   160	    val.x = adjust_lon(t.x + ct.ll[0]);
   161	    val.y = t.y + ct.ll[1];
   162	  } else {
   163	    if (!isNaN(t.x)) {
   164	      val.x = pin.x + t.x;
   165	      val.y = pin.y + t.y;
   166	    }
   167	  }
   168	  return val;
   169	}
   170

     1	'use strict';
     2	import { PJD_3PARAM, PJD_7PARAM, HALF_PI } from './constants/values';
     3	export function compareDatums(source, dest) {
     4	  if (source.datum_type !== dest.datum_type) {
     5	    return false; // false, datums are not equal
     6	  } else if (source.a !== dest.a || Math.abs(source.es - dest.es) > 0.000000000050) {
     7	    // the tolerance for es is to ensure that GRS80 and WGS84
     8	    // are considered identical
     9	    return false;
    10	  } else if (source.datum_type === PJD_3PARAM) {
    11	    return (source.datum_params[0] === dest.datum_params[0] && source.datum_params[1] === dest.datum_params[1] && source.datum_params[2] === dest.datum_params[2]);
    12	  } else if (source.datum_type === PJD_7PARAM) {
    13	    return (source.datum_params[0] === dest.datum_params[0] && source.datum_params[1] === dest.datum_params[1] && source.datum_params[2] === dest.datum_params[2] && source.datum_params[3] === dest.datum_params[3] && source.datum_params[4] === dest.datum_params[4] && source.datum_params[5] === dest.datum_params[5] && source.datum_params[6] === dest.datum_params[6]);
    14	  } else {
    15	    return true; // datums are equal
    16	  }
    17	} // cs_compare_datums()
    18	
    19	/*
    20	 * The function Convert_Geodetic_To_Geocentric converts geodetic coordinates
    21	 * (latitude, longitude, and height) to geocentric coordinates (X, Y, Z),
    22	 * according to the current ellipsoid parameters.
    23	 *
    24	 *    Latitude  : Geodetic latitude in radians                     (input)
    25	 *    Longitude : Geodetic longitude in radians                    (input)
    26	 *    Height    : Geodetic height, in meters                       (input)
    27	 *    X         : Calculated Geocentric X coordinate, in meters    (output)
    28	 *    Y         : Calculated Geocentric Y coordinate, in meters    (output)
    29	 *    Z         : Calculated Geocentric Z coordinate, in meters    (output)
    30	 *
    31	 */
    32	export function geodeticToGeocentric(p, es, a) {
    33	  var Longitude = p.x;
    34	  var Latitude = p.y;
    35	  var Height = p.z ? p.z : 0; // Z value not always supplied
    36	
    37	  var Rn; /*  Earth radius at location  */
    38	  var Sin_Lat; /*  Math.sin(Latitude)  */
    39	  var Sin2_Lat; /*  Square of Math.sin(Latitude)  */
    40	  var Cos_Lat; /*  Math.cos(Latitude)  */
    41	
    42	  /*
    43	   ** Don't blow up if Latitude is just a little out of the value
    44	   ** range as it may just be a rounding issue.  Also removed longitude
    45	   ** test, it should be wrapped by Math.cos() and Math.sin().  NFW for PROJ.4, Sep/2001.
    46	   */
    47	  if (Latitude < -HALF_PI && Latitude > -1.001 * HALF_PI) {
    48	    Latitude = -HALF_PI;
    49	  } else if (Latitude > HALF_PI && Latitude < 1.001 * HALF_PI) {
    50	    Latitude = HALF_PI;
    51	  } else if (Latitude < -HALF_PI) {
    52	    /* Latitude out of range */
    53	    // ..reportError('geocent:lat out of range:' + Latitude);
    54	    return { x: -Infinity, y: -Infinity, z: p.z };
    55	  } else if (Latitude > HALF_PI) {
    56	    /* Latitude out of range */
    57	    return { x: Infinity, y: Infinity, z: p.z };
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  if (Longitude > Math.PI) {
    61	    Longitude -= (2 * Math.PI);
    62	  }
    63	  Sin_Lat = Math.sin(Latitude);
    64	  Cos_Lat = Math.cos(Latitude);
    65	  Sin2_Lat = Sin_Lat * Sin_Lat;
    66	  Rn = a / (Math.sqrt(1.0e0 - es * Sin2_Lat));
    67	  return {
    68	    x: (Rn + Height) * Cos_Lat * Math.cos(Longitude),
    69	    y: (Rn + Height) * Cos_Lat * Math.sin(Longitude),
    70	    z: ((Rn * (1 - es)) + Height) * Sin_Lat
    71	  };
    72	} // cs_geodetic_to_geocentric()
    73	
    74	export function geocentricToGeodetic(p, es, a, b) {
    75	  /* local defintions and variables */
    76	  /* end-criterium of loop, accuracy of sin(Latitude) */
    77	  var genau = 1e-12;
    78	  var genau2 = (genau * genau);
    79	  var maxiter = 30;
    80	
    81	  var P; /* distance between semi-minor axis and location */
    82	  var RR; /* distance between center and location */
    83	  var CT; /* sin of geocentric latitude */
    84	  var ST; /* cos of geocentric latitude */
    85	  var RX;
    86	  var RK;
    87	  var RN; /* Earth radius at location */
    88	  var CPHI0; /* cos of start or old geodetic latitude in iterations */
    89	  var SPHI0; /* sin of start or old geodetic latitude in iterations */
    90	  var CPHI; /* cos of searched geodetic latitude */
    91	  var SPHI; /* sin of searched geodetic latitude */
    92	  var SDPHI; /* end-criterium: addition-theorem of sin(Latitude(iter)-Latitude(iter-1)) */
    93	  var iter; /* # of continous iteration, max. 30 is always enough (s.a.) */
    94	
    95	  var X = p.x;
    96	  var Y = p.y;
    97	  var Z = p.z ? p.z : 0.0; // Z value not always supplied
    98	  var Longitude;
    99	  var Latitude;
   100	  var Height;
   101	
   102	  P = Math.sqrt(X * X + Y * Y);
   103	  RR = Math.sqrt(X * X + Y * Y + Z * Z);
   104	
   105	  /*      special cases for latitude and longitude */
   106	  if (P / a < genau) {
   107	    /*  special case, if P=0. (X=0., Y=0.) */
   108	    Longitude = 0.0;
   109	
   110	    /*  if (X,Y,Z)=(0.,0.,0.) then Height becomes semi-minor axis
   111	     *  of ellipsoid (=center of mass), Latitude becomes PI/2 */
   112	    if (RR / a < genau) {
   113	      Latitude = HALF_PI;
   114	      Height = -b;
   115	      return {
   116	        x: p.x,
   117	        y: p.y,
   118	        z: p.z
   119	      };
   120	    }
   121	  } else {
   122	    /*  ellipsoidal (geodetic) longitude
   123	     *  interval: -PI < Longitude <= +PI */
   124	    Longitude = Math.atan2(Y, X);
   125	  }
   126	
   127	  /* --------------------------------------------------------------
   128	   * Following iterative algorithm was developped by
   129	   * "Institut for Erdmessung", University of Hannover, July 1988.
   130	   * Internet: www.ife.uni-hannover.de
   131	   * Iterative computation of CPHI,SPHI and Height.
   132	   * Iteration of CPHI and SPHI to 10**-12 radian resp.
   133	   * 2*10**-7 arcsec.
   134	   * --------------------------------------------------------------
   135	   */
   136	  CT = Z / RR;
   137	  ST = P / RR;
   138	  RX = 1.0 / Math.sqrt(1.0 - es * (2.0 - es) * ST * ST);
   139	  CPHI0 = ST * (1.0 - es) * RX;
   140	  SPHI0 = CT * RX;
   141	  iter = 0;
   142	
   143	  /* loop to find sin(Latitude) resp. Latitude
   144	   * until |sin(Latitude(iter)-Latitude(iter-1))| < genau */
   145	  do {
   146	    iter++;
   147	    RN = a / Math.sqrt(1.0 - es * SPHI0 * SPHI0);
   148	
   149	    /*  ellipsoidal (geodetic) height */
   150	    Height = P * CPHI0 + Z * SPHI0 - RN * (1.0 - es * SPHI0 * SPHI0);
   151	
   152	    RK = es * RN / (RN + Height);
   153	    RX = 1.0 / Math.sqrt(1.0 - RK * (2.0 - RK) * ST * ST);
   154	    CPHI = ST * (1.0 - RK) * RX;
   155	    SPHI = CT * RX;
   156	    SDPHI = SPHI * CPHI0 - CPHI * SPHI0;
   157	    CPHI0 = CPHI;
   158	    SPHI0 = SPHI;
   159	  }
   160	  while (SDPHI * SDPHI > genau2 && iter < maxiter);
   161	
   162	  /*      ellipsoidal (geodetic) latitude */
   163	  Latitude = Math.atan(SPHI / Math.abs(CPHI));
   164	  return {
   165	    x: Longitude,
   166	    y: Latitude,
   167	    z: Height
   168	  };
   169	} // cs_geocentric_to_geodetic()
   170	
   171	/****************************************************************/
   172	// pj_geocentic_to_wgs84( p )
   173	//  p = point to transform in geocentric coordinates (x,y,z)
   174	
   175	/** point object, nothing fancy, just allows values to be
   176	    passed back and forth by reference rather than by value.
   177	    Other point classes may be used as long as they have
   178	    x and y properties, which will get modified in the transform method.
   179	*/
   180	export function geocentricToWgs84(p, datum_type, datum_params) {
